# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 00:41:46.681708

### Base Program

```py
def count_square_triples(n):
    count = 0
    for a in range(1, n + 1):
        for b in range(a, n + 1):
            c = int((a * a + b * b)**0.5)
            if c * c == a * a + b * b and c <= n:
                count += 1
    return count
```

### Input

```json
[6]
```


## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def count_square_triples(n):
    count = 0
    for a in range(1, n + 1):
        for b in range(a, n + 1):
            c = int((a * a + b * b) ** 0.5)
            if c * c == a * a + b * b and c <= n:
                count += 1
    return count
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def count_square_triples(var_0):
    count = 0
    for a in range(1, var_0 + 1):
        for b in range(a, var_0 + 1):
            c = int((a * a + b * b) ** 0.5)
            if c * c == a * a + b * b and c <= var_0:
                count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def count_square_triples(n):
    count = 0
    for a in range(1, 1 + n):
        for b in range(a, 1 + n):
            c = int((b * b + a * a) ** 0.5)
            if c * c == b * b + a * a and c <= n:
                count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def count_square_triples(var_1):
    count = 0
    for a in range(1, 1 + var_1):
        for b in range(a, 1 + var_1):
            c = int((b * b + a * a) ** 0.5)
            if c * c == b * b + a * a and c <= var_1:
                count += 1
    return count
```
